1317 = {
	name= "Орис"  # Baratheon rumoured half-brother of Aegon the Conqueror.
	dynasty=498
	
	dna="bfcfecbikak"
	properties="ac0ack"
	
	martial = 13
	diplomacy = 8
	intrigue = 4
	stewardship = 10
	learning = 6

	religion = valyrian_rel
	culture="western_valyrian"
	
	add_trait="skilled_tactician"
	add_trait="bastard"
	add_trait="strong"
	add_trait="honorable"
	add_trait="gregarious"
	add_trait="authoritative"
	add_trait="brave"
	add_trait="diligent"
	
	father=77064
	employer=77064

	7978.1.1 = {
		birth="7978.1.1" 
		add_trait=assign_mission_target #cadet dynasty tracker, baratheon
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { dynasty = 317 } }
				set_dynasty_flag = is_cadet_house
				c_77064 = { #targaryen father
					set_dynasty_flag = has_cadet_house
					set_dynasty_flag = owned_cadet_house_@PREV
					ROOT = { set_dynasty_flag = cadet_house_@PREV }
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	7994.1.1 = {
	    add_trait="duelist"
		add_trait="master_warrior"
	}
	7996.1.1={
		employer = 77000
	}	
	7998.2.27={
		effect = { 
			set_government_type = feudal_government #to prevent him being called Archon for some reason
			set_government_type = feudal_government_LP
		} 
	}
	7998.2.28= {
		add_spouse=11544
		dynasty=317
		#remove_trait="bastard"
		#add_trait="legit_bastard"
		remove_trait=assign_mission_target #no longer cadet house
		effect = { 
			set_dynasty_flag = has_traditional_names
			d_dragonstone = { remove_claim = ROOT }
			c_dragonstone = { remove_claim = ROOT }
		}
	}
	8000.1.1 = {
		add_trait = knight # Knighted at Aegon took Oldtown.
		religion=the_seven
		culture="stormlander"
	} 
	8004.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
				add_trait = one_handed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" } }
				add_trait = disfigured_AGOT
			}
		}	
		give_nickname = nick_one_hand
		add_trait = wroth #was said to have become crabbed and bitter
		add_trait = cruel
		remove_trait = gregarious
		remove_trait = honorable
	} 
	8038.4.3 ={ # Died of wounds during Vulture Hunt
		add_trait = wounded
		add_trait = one_handed
		death= {death_reason = death_trait}
	} 
}

		effect={
			e_iron_throne= {
				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { imprison = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			set_defacto_liege = ROOT
			set_character_flag = against_king
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}				
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 8 } #stormlands
			}
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
						years = 20
					}
				}
			}
			c_dragonstone = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					ROOT = {
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8129.8.1 = {death = {
			death_reason = death_execution
			killer = 77013
		} 
	}
}
